msg:1. The room was not cleaned thoroughly. There were items left behind by the previous tenants. After checking out, I gave feedback to the housekeeper. The cleaning lady also asked me to write a thank you note. I politely refused, so she was a little rude. The hotel does not need to use good reviews as an evaluation indicator. It should really consider things from the perspective of the guests. Sincere service can make customers feel comfortable and caring. Before checking in, I called in advance to contact the guy who had other needs and the guy who helped to get takeout and communicate at night. The service was pretty good and handled things neatly.
2. On the first day of check-in, I went to have breakfast. The auntie who cooked noodles had a bad attitude and was "forgetful". I ordered beef noodles. She told me not to stand and wait, just go around and come back. When I went around to get the noodles, a lady happened to say that she wanted beef noodles, and then gave the cooked noodles to the lady who came later. Then she looked up and saw me and asked me again what I wanted? Slightly speechless, it turned out that I just ordered for nothing. So I ordered again and didn't go to have breakfast the next day.
3. The hotel's featured project, Amber's 24-hour mansion butler service: To be honest, it's very ordinary. I feel like they are not the same person. They speak in different tones and are not familiar with their duties. They answered questions that were not asked (I asked about the check-out time, and he told me the kitchen's off-get off work time, um...) and they also said the wrong last name. Based on the nature of my job, I often travel on business, and I have basically tried various hotels and homestays both abroad and domestically. This 24-hour butler service has also been experienced in other hotels, and it is more meticulous, decent and complete. The so-called most luxurious and only hotel in Guiyang has very ordinary service, and at most it can be given a satisfactory evaluation. It is still a long way from the real luxury. There is no welcoming guest in front of the door, and there is no service staff to help with luggage.
4. Taking a taxi back to the hotel will never be at the main entrance, but on the side of the hotel, and you need to walk a distance by yourself. It is said that it was under renovation before, but local drivers default to the previous location route.
5. The hotel air conditioner can only cool but not heat. The weather in Guiyang has been unpredictable in the past few days. It was suddenly very cold. It was very cold when I slept at night, and then I caught a cold. I consulted the housekeeper, who replied that the central air conditioning was controlled and could not heat, and then gave me a heater. After chatting for a while, the housekeeper said, "There are guests who feel hot and need to lower the temperature." This fact cannot be verified, but I think that in this weather, anyone with normal perception should not feel hot.
